     1	# AGENT_REINITIALIZATION.md
     2	
     3	Last refreshed: 2026-05-28
     4	Maintainer scope: AI coding agents and senior engineers onboarding quickly
     5	Source policy: Every project-specific statement is tagged `[VERIFIED]` or `[INFERRED]`
     6	
     7	---
     8	
     9	## Investigation Summary
    10	
    11	- The highest-churn files across history are `src/services/veniceClient.ts`, `src/modules/SettingsModule.tsx`, `server.ts`, `electron/main.ts`, and `src/App.tsx`; this is where behavioral risk concentrates. `[VERIFIED]`
    12	- The project has shifted from early web-proxy-first architecture to direct IPC transport in Electron, with shared validation (`src/shared/validation.ts`) used by both IPC and web proxy paths. `[VERIFIED]`
    13	- Packaging and release automation now targets both Windows and macOS, with artifact verification and SHA-256 checksums in workflows and scripts. `[VERIFIED]`
    14	- Current lint posture allows warnings and enforces a budget gate via `npm run lint:eslint` (`--max-warnings=96`), while strict TypeScript remains enabled in both renderer and Electron configs. `[VERIFIED]`
    15	- There is no existing `AGENT_REINITIALIZATION.md` in the repo; `AGENTS.md` is the current long-form agent guide and has been superseded by this file for deep context. `[VERIFIED]`
    16	
    17	---
    18	
    19	## 1) Current High-Level Architecture & Mental Model
    20	
    21	### 1.1 Dominant mental model
    22	
    23	- Venice Forge is a dual-mode app:
    24	  - Electron desktop mode (production-oriented).
    25	  - Browser web mode (development-oriented). `[VERIFIED]`
    26	- The renderer codebase is shared; transport is the key mode switch:
    27	  - Electron: renderer -> preload bridge -> IPC handlers -> main-process Venice HTTPS client.
    28	  - Web: renderer -> Express proxy `/api/venice/*` -> Venice HTTPS API. `[VERIFIED]`
    29	- Security boundaries are explicit:
    30	  - Renderer has no Node.js access in Electron (`contextIsolation: true`, `nodeIntegration: false`, `sandbox: true`).
    31	  - Allowed endpoints/methods are constrained in shared validation. `[VERIFIED]`
    32	
    33	### 1.2 Runtime flow (real modules only)
    34	
    35	```mermaid
    36	flowchart LR
    37	  UI[React Renderer src/*] --> VC[src/services/veniceClient.ts]
    38	  VC -->|Electron mode| DBR[src/services/desktopBridge.ts]
    39	  DBR --> PRE[electron/preload.ts]
    40	  PRE --> IPC[electron/ipc/handlers.ts]
    41	  IPC --> VAL[electron/ipc/validation.ts]
    42	  IPC --> MCLI[electron/services/veniceClient.ts]
    43	  MCLI --> VENICE[(api.venice.ai)]
    44	
    45	  VC -->|Web mode| PROXY[server.ts /api/venice]
    46	  PROXY --> SVAL[src/shared/validation.ts]
    47	  PROXY --> VENICE
    48	
    49	  UI --> STORE[src/services/storageService.ts]
    50	  STORE --> IDB[(IndexedDB)]
    51	  IPC --> SSTORE[electron/services/secureStore.ts]
    52	  SSTORE --> OSSEC[(OS secure storage)]
    53	```
    54	
    55	All nodes above exist as concrete files in repo. `[VERIFIED]`
    56	
    57	### 1.3 Core data flows
    58	
    59	| Flow | Primary files | Invariants |
    60	|---|---|---|
    61	| API request/response | `src/services/veniceClient.ts`, `src/shared/validation.ts`, `electron/ipc/validation.ts`, `server.ts` | Only allowlisted endpoints and methods are accepted; retry logic targets `429/500/503`. `[VERIFIED]` |
    62	| Streaming chat | `src/services/veniceClient.ts`, `electron/preload.ts`, `electron/ipc/handlers.ts`, `electron/services/veniceClient.ts` | Streaming only for `POST /chat/completions`; delta transport keyed by `signalId`. `[VERIFIED]` |
    63	| Local state lifecycle | `src/App.tsx`, `src/state/appReducer.ts`, modules in `src/modules/` | One global reducer; modules receive `{ state, dispatch }`; settings persisted into IndexedDB. `[VERIFIED]` |
    64	| Persistent local data | `src/services/storageService.ts`, `src/services/cryptoService.ts`, `src/services/exportImport.ts` | Store set is controlled by `STORE_NAMES`; encrypted wrapper used for selected stores; import/export size-limited and schema-checked. `[VERIFIED]` |
    65	| API key lifecycle | `electron/services/secureStore.ts`, `electron/ipc/handlers.ts`, `src/services/desktopBridge.ts` | Desktop mode stores key in safeStorage-backed file; renderer cannot read raw key. `[VERIFIED]` |
    66	| Diagnostics/logging | `src/services/veniceClient.ts`, `src/modules/DiagnosticsModule.tsx`, `electron/services/logger.ts` | Request diagnostics emitted via reducer actions; logs redact sensitive values. `[VERIFIED]` |
    67	
    68	### 1.4 Architecture invariants that matter for edits
    69	
    70	- Renderer modules should call `veniceFetch`/`veniceStreamChat`; not direct `fetch('/api/venice/...')` in module code. `[VERIFIED]`
    71	- Any new Venice endpoint requires updates in both shared allowlist and IPC validation gate (and proxy behavior if web mode needed). `[VERIFIED]`
    72	- Any new IPC feature requires preload + IPC handler + validation + desktop bridge surface alignment. `[VERIFIED]`
    73	- Global state shape and mutation semantics are reducer-driven; side effects sit in services/modules. `[VERIFIED]`
    74	
    75	---
    76	
    77	## 2) Key Domain Concepts & Business Logic
    78	
    79	### 2.1 Domain vocabulary
    80	
    81	| Concept | Meaning in this codebase | Where encoded |
    82	|---|---|---|
    83	| Dual mode | Same renderer running either against IPC or web proxy transport | `src/services/desktopBridge.ts`, `src/services/veniceClient.ts`, `server.ts` |
    84	| Venice request allowlist | Explicit endpoint + method allowlist, pair-validated | `src/shared/validation.ts`, `electron/ipc/validation.ts`, `server.ts` |
    85	| Fallback models | Built-in models used when live model fetch unavailable | `src/constants/venice.ts`, `src/state/appReducer.ts` |
    86	| Diagnostics entry | Per-request metadata record in reducer log | `src/services/veniceClient.ts`, `src/state/appReducer.ts` |
    87	| Encrypted IndexedDB wrappers | Stored object with `{ id, timestamp, data, _isEncryptedWrapper }` for encrypted stores | `src/services/storageService.ts` |
    88	| Export envelope | `{ version, exportedAt, appVersion, data }` payload with filtered stores | `src/services/exportImport.ts` |
    89	
    90	All concept mappings above are directly visible in file implementations. `[VERIFIED]`
    91	
    92	### 2.2 Business logic that is easy to break
    93	
    94	- Model selection is auto-corrected when a previously selected model disappears after refresh; reducer emits warning toasts and switches selection. `[VERIFIED]`
    95	- Web chat search toggle (`webSearch`) has legacy coercion behavior (`boolean` -> enum string) to avoid malformed payload regressions. `[VERIFIED]`
    96	- Upload handling includes raw-byte and serialized-byte boundaries; serializer estimates base64 overhead. `[VERIFIED]`
    97	- Decrypt failures are intentionally non-fatal: records are skipped and warning surfaced; app continues loading remaining data. `[VERIFIED]`
    98	
    99	### 2.3 Product-level assumptions inferred from code
   100	
   101	- Desktop mode is treated as the “real” secure transport, while web mode exists primarily for development/test convenience. `[INFERRED]`
   102	- The project optimizes for resilience and user continuity over hard-fail behavior when local persisted records become unreadable. `[INFERRED]`
   103	
   104	---
   105	
   106	## 3) Major Recent Changes & Architectural Decisions
   107	
   108	Grounding: derived from `git log --oneline -50` plus commit stats/details.
   109	
   110	| Change | Date/Commit | Why | Tradeoff | Impact on agents |
   111	|---|---|---|---|---|
   112	| Refactor UI styles and accessibility | 2026-05-28 `b18b853` | Consolidate styling/a11y improvements and remove legacy CSS cruft | Large UI diffs increase merge conflict risk in modules/components | Avoid broad UI rewrites in same PR as logic fixes; keep behavioral edits isolated. `[VERIFIED]` |
   113	| Tailwind Premium Dark Glass migration | 2026-05-28 `f87025a` | Move to utility-first UI styling and consistent aesthetic | Large CSS/JSX churn; class-heavy diffs are noisy | Prefer existing Tailwind patterns; do not reintroduce old CSS abstractions. `[VERIFIED]` |
   114	| Focus trap and modal accessibility hardening | 2026-05-28 `de01def` | Close keyboard/ARIA gaps and unify modal behavior | Additional hook coupling and event ordering complexity | Reuse `useFocusTrap`; avoid ad hoc modal key handlers. `[VERIFIED]` |
   115	| Central AppConfig schema introduced | 2026-05-28 `a4f5a19` | Consolidate env parsing and validation | Indirection can hide runtime defaults | Read `src/shared/configSchema.ts` before adding env vars; keep bounds explicit. `[VERIFIED]` |
   116	| Auto-update integration (`electron-updater`) | 2026-05-28 `22b7cdc` | Add in-app update checks/download/install flow | More IPC surface + release workflow complexity | New update channels must be wired across preload/bridge/UI/tests. `[VERIFIED]` |
   117	| macOS release support and verification | 2026-05-28 `6a9b740`, `a8c8c9b` | Dual-platform packaging and artifact checks | More CI branches and signing paths | Validate platform-specific scripts/workflows before release changes. `[VERIFIED]` |
   118	| Endpoint-method pair enforcement | 2026-05-22 `9385d66` | Prevent method misuse on allowlisted endpoints | Slightly stricter behavior may break permissive clients | Keep `VENICE_ENDPOINT_METHODS` authoritative and synced. `[VERIFIED]` |
   119	| Web mode key handling switched server-side | 2026-05-23 `6af3f1b` | Prevent web renderer local key usage | Web mode cannot test arbitrary user keys from UI | Don’t add web local key storage without explicit security decision. `[VERIFIED]` |
   120	| Direct IPC transport hardened in Electron | 2026-05-20 `3f0f15c` | Remove loopback proxy dependence in desktop mode | More main-process complexity | Treat IPC validation as security boundary; tests are non-optional for changes. `[VERIFIED]` |
   121	| Electron migration from web-only app | 2026-05-20 `fefd60f` (+ merge `c86985a`) | Desktop distribution + secure storage + release packaging | Increased code surface and dual-runtime complexity | Always reason by runtime mode; browser-only assumptions are often wrong. `[VERIFIED]` |
   122	
   123	No structural change claims above are based on unstated PR metadata. `[VERIFIED]`
   124

   130

   133	| `src/` | Renderer app: modules, state, services, shared TS types/utilities. `[VERIFIED]` |

   136	| `.github/workflows/` | CI + Windows release + macOS release pipelines. `[VERIFIED]` |
   137	| `scripts/` | Build/release support (icon generation, dist verification, checksums, CJS package shim). `[VERIFIED]` |
   138	| `docs/` | Release/security/platform/support documentation. `[VERIFIED]` |

   140	### 4.2 Critical file ownership map (practical, not exhaustive)
   141	
   142	| File | Role | Edit risk |
   143	|---|---|---|
   144	| `src/services/veniceClient.ts` | Transport abstraction + retries + diagnostics + stream parsing + form serialization | Very high |
   145	| `src/state/appReducer.ts` | Global state transitions and model fallback behavior | High |
   146	| `src/App.tsx` | App bootstrapping, hydration, bridge init, tab routing | High |
   147	| `electron/main.ts` | Window security settings, CSP, navigation policy | Very high |
   148	| `electron/ipc/validation.ts` | Main security gate for renderer->main requests | Very high |
   149	| `electron/ipc/handlers.ts` | IPC endpoint bindings + diagnostics/files/update wiring | High |
   150	| `server.ts` | Web mode security and transport controls | Very high |
   151	| `src/services/storageService.ts` | IndexedDB encryption wrapper, decrypt-failure handling | High |

   164	
   165	## 5) Core Patterns, Conventions & Coding Standards
   166	
   167	### 5.1 Patterns enforced by code structure
   168	
   169	- Global state is reducer-centric (`useReducer` + Immer) with discriminated actions. `[VERIFIED]`
   170	- Module components are function declarations in `src/modules/`; services hold transport/storage logic. `[VERIFIED]`
   171	- Desktop-vs-web behavior should be routed through bridge/client abstractions (`isElectron`, `desktop*` wrappers), not scattered runtime checks everywhere. `[VERIFIED]`
   172	- Safety gates are layered:
   173	  - shared validation allowlist;
   174	  - main-process IPC validation;
   175	  - proxy validation for web mode. `[VERIFIED]`
   176	
   177	### 5.2 Error-handling conventions
   178	
   179	- Renderer transport normalizes HTTP/API errors to user-facing strings and diagnostics entries. `[VERIFIED]`
   180	- IPC handler failures are sanitized (`redactErrorMessage`) before returning to renderer. `[VERIFIED]`
   181	- Import/export and storage failures use non-destructive behavior with toasts/warnings where feasible. `[VERIFIED]`
   182	
   183	### 5.3 Testing conventions that are encoded
   184	
   185	- Default Vitest environment is `jsdom`; server tests explicitly mark node env. `[VERIFIED]`
   186	- Regression markers use `BUG-###` comments in tests. `[VERIFIED]`
   187	- CI runs `lint:eslint`, `typecheck`, `test`, `build`; local `ci` script runs the same steps. `[VERIFIED]`
   188	
   189	### 5.4 Concrete “good pattern” examples (copied from repository logic)
   190	
   191	Example A: dual-layer endpoint/method validation.
   192	
   193	```ts
   194	// src/shared/validation.ts
   195	export const VENICE_ENDPOINT_METHODS = {
   196	  "/models": ["GET"],
   197	  "/chat/completions": ["POST"],
   198	  "/image/generate": ["POST"],
   199	  "/image/upscale": ["POST"],
   200	  "/augment/search": ["POST"],
   201	  "/augment/scrape": ["POST"],
   202	  "/augment/text-parser": ["POST"],
   203	};
   204	```
   205	
   206	Why it is good:
   207	- Shared source of truth consumed by both server and IPC validation, reducing drift risk. `[VERIFIED]`
   208	
   209	Example B: reducer guard against malformed settings payloads.
   210	
   211	```ts
   212	// src/state/appReducer.ts
   213	if (!action.settings || typeof action.settings !== "object" || Array.isArray(action.settings)) break;
   214	const allowedKeys = ["defaultSystemPrompt", "includeVeniceSystemPrompt", "webSearch", "webScraping", "webCitations", "theme", "customModels"];
   215	```
   216	
   217	Why it is good:
   218	- Prevents crashes/prototype abuse from malformed imported settings while preserving backward compatibility. `[VERIFIED]`
   219	
   220	---

   222	## 6) Important Abstractions, Frameworks, Libraries & Tech Stack
   223	
   224	### 6.1 Pinned runtime/tool versions from lockfile
   225	
   226	Data source: `package-lock.json` entries under `node_modules/*`.
   227	
   228	| Library | Locked version |
   229	|---|---|
   230	| `react` | `19.2.6` |
   231	| `react-dom` | `19.2.6` |
   232	| `electron` | `42.3.0` |
   233	| `electron-builder` | `26.8.1` |
   234	| `electron-updater` | `6.8.3` |
   235	| `vite` | `6.4.2` |
   236	| `vitest` | `4.1.7` |
   237	| `typescript` | `5.8.3` |
   238	| `tailwindcss` | `4.3.0` |
   239	| `express` | `4.22.2` |
   240	| `http-proxy-middleware` | `4.0.0` |
   241	| `immer` | `11.1.8` |
   242	| `eslint` | `9.39.4` |
   243	
   244	All above are lockfile-grounded, not semver ranges from `package.json`. `[VERIFIED]`
   245	
   246	### 6.2 Abstractions you should treat as contracts
   247	
   248	| Abstraction | Contract |
   249	|---|---|
   250	| `veniceFetch` / `veniceStreamChat` | Renderer’s only transport API; emits diagnostics and handles retries/abort semantics. `[VERIFIED]` |
   251	| `desktopBridge` | Mode abstraction layer; web-safe no-op behavior for desktop-only APIs. `[VERIFIED]` |
   252	| `StorageService` | Typed store names + encryption wrapper for protected stores + metadata-returning reads. `[VERIFIED]` |
   253	| `AppConfig` | Env parsing/bounds with defaults; source for proxy/body/rate settings. `[VERIFIED]` |
   254	| Shared limits (`src/shared/limits.ts`) | Single source for 25 MiB bounds and upload serialization ceilings across layers. `[VERIFIED]` |
   255	
   256	### 6.3 Why these choices appear to have been made
   257	
   258	- Shared validation + limits reduce transport drift bugs across IPC/web/import flows. `[INFERRED]`
   259	- Direct IPC in desktop mode keeps API key out of renderer and avoids local HTTP attack surface. `[INFERRED]`
   260	- Tailwind migration likely optimizes velocity in large UI updates compared to hand-maintained CSS files. `[INFERRED]`
   261

   285

   287	- In mixed UI+logic files, split commits by concern to avoid unreviewable diffs. `[INFERRED]`

   289	---
   290	
   291	## 8) Common Pitfalls & Anti-Patterns to Avoid
   292	
   293	Grounded in TODOs, regression tests, and bug-fix history.
   294	
   295	### 8.1 Transport and validation pitfalls
   296	
   297	- Adding a new endpoint in one place only (e.g., proxy but not IPC validation) causes mode divergence and runtime failures. `[VERIFIED]`
   298	- Sending request bodies with GET is explicitly blocked in validation paths. `[VERIFIED]`
   299	- Trusting renderer headers (`authorization`, `host`, `cookie`) is forbidden; they are stripped. `[VERIFIED]`
   300	
   301	### 8.2 Storage/import pitfalls
   302	
   303	- Treating decrypt failure as hard error blocks app startup unnecessarily; current behavior intentionally skips unreadable records and warns. `[VERIFIED]`
   304	- Writing to arbitrary stores is restricted by typed store names and known constants; bypassing this increases data corruption risk. `[VERIFIED]`
   305	- Import/export size limit is shared (25 MiB) and should remain unified with IPC/proxy constants. `[VERIFIED]`
   306	
   307	### 8.3 UI/module pitfalls from past regressions
   308	
   309	- Chat/image async flows previously had unsafe `finally` return behavior; avoid `return` inside `finally` blocks. `[VERIFIED]`
   310	- Legacy boolean `webSearch` values caused malformed payloads; always normalize through reducer/payload builders. `[VERIFIED]`
   311	- Placeholder UI states inserted into real chat messages can leak into API payload context; use toasts/status state instead. `[VERIFIED]`
   312	
   313	### 8.4 Release/CI pitfalls
   314	
   315	- CI workflow (`.github/workflows/ci.yml`) runs `npm run lint:eslint` alongside `typecheck`, `test`, and `build`. `[VERIFIED]`
   316	- Public tag release workflows enforce signing secret presence; test dispatch runs have different env expectations. `[VERIFIED]`
   317	
   318	### 8.5 Explicit anti-pattern list
   319	
   320	- Direct module fetches to `/api/venice/*` bypassing `veniceClient`. `[VERIFIED]`
   321	- Direct `window.veniceForge` calls inside modules instead of `desktopBridge`/client wrappers. `[VERIFIED]`
   322	- Expanding `any` usage in already high-churn files without adding narrowing/guards. `[VERIFIED]`
   323	- Mixing large visual restyles with transport/security changes in one commit. `[INFERRED]`
   324	
   325	---

   328	
   329	All commands below are copied from `package.json` scripts unless noted.
   330	
   331	### 9.1 Canonical command table
   332	
   333	| Purpose | Command |
   334	|---|---|
   335	| Dev server (web mode) | `npm run dev:web` |
   336	| Dev app (Electron mode) | `npm run dev:electron` |
   337	| Build all | `npm run build` |
   338	| Build renderer only | `npm run build:web` |
   339	| Build proxy server bundle | `npm run build:server` |
   340	| Build Electron main | `npm run build:electron` |
   341	| Typecheck renderer + Electron | `npm run typecheck` |
   342	| TS-only lint alias | `npm run lint` |
   343	| ESLint gate | `npm run lint:eslint` |
   344	| Unit/integration tests | `npm test` |
   345	| Watch tests | `npm run test:watch` |
   346	| Coverage | `npm run test:coverage` |
   347	| Electron smoke test | `npm run smoke:electron` |
   348	| Package default | `npm run dist` |
   349	| Package Windows | `npm run dist:win` |
   350	| Package Windows portable | `npm run dist:portable` |
   351	| Package macOS universal workflow | `npm run dist:mac` |
   352	| Package macOS arm64 only | `npm run dist:mac:arm64` |
   353	| Package macOS x64 only | `npm run dist:mac:x64` |
   354	| Verify icon assets | `npm run verify:icon` |
   355	| Verify release artifacts (dispatcher) | `npm run verify:dist` |
   356	| Verify Windows artifacts | `npm run verify:dist:win` |
   357	| Verify macOS artifacts | `npm run verify:dist:mac` |
   358	| Generate release checksums | `npm run checksum:release` |
   359	| Full local CI command | `npm run ci` |
   360	| Clean generated artifacts | `npm run clean` |
   361	
   362	### 9.2 CI workflows (exact behavior today)
   363	
   364	| Workflow | Trigger | Node | Core steps |
   365	|---|---|---|---|
   366	| `ci.yml` | push/PR on `main` | matrix `20.x`, `22.x` | `npm ci --prefer-offline` -> `npm run lint:eslint` -> `npm run typecheck` -> `npm test` -> `npm run build` |
   367	| `windows-release.yml` | tag `v*` or dispatch | `22` | install -> verify icon -> typecheck -> test -> build -> dist win -> checksum -> verify dist win -> upload/publish |
   368	| `macos-release.yml` | tag `v*` or dispatch | `22` | install -> verify icon -> typecheck -> test -> build -> dist mac -> checksum -> verify dist mac -> upload/publish |
   369	
   370	Observations:
   371	- `ci.yml` calls `npm run lint:eslint`. `[VERIFIED]`
   372	- Release workflows enforce signing/notarization credentials only for tag-based public releases. `[VERIFIED]`
   373	
   374	### 9.3 Key environment variables in active use
   375	
   376	| Variable | Used in | Purpose |
   377	|---|---|---|
   378	| `VENICE_API_KEY` | `server.ts`/config schema | Server-side key for web proxy mode |
   379	| `PORT` | `server.ts`/config schema | Express bind port |
   380	| `RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS` | `server.ts`/config schema | Rate-limit window |
   381	| `RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS` | `server.ts`/config schema | Per-IP request cap |
   382	| `MAX_PROXY_BODY_BYTES` | config schema | Proxy raw body limit, bounded by shared max |
   383	| `TRUST_PROXY` | `server.ts` | Optional Express `trust proxy` setting |
   384	| `DISABLE_HMR` | `vite.config.ts` | Disable Vite HMR |
   385	| `ELECTRON_BUILD` | `vite.config.ts` | Relative asset base for Electron build |
   386	| `VENICE_FORGE_DEBUG_DEVTOOLS` | `electron/main.ts` | Allow devtools in packaged app |
   387	| `VENICE_FORGE_ALLOW_PLAINTEXT_KEY_STORAGE` | secure store service | Allow plaintext fallback outside Windows scope |
   388	
   389	### 9.4 Known command policy mismatches
   390	
   391	| Mismatch | Repo evidence | Recommendation impact |
   392	|---|---|---|
   393	| Root docs mention “full CI pipeline includes lint” in some places, but GitHub `ci.yml` omits ESLint step | `AGENTS.md` narrative vs `.github/workflows/ci.yml` commands | Agent changes that rely on lint gate should run `npm run lint:eslint` locally until CI is aligned. `[VERIFIED]` |

   396	
   397	## 10) Living Document Protocol
   398	
   399	This file is intended as the deep context source for future agent sessions.
   400	
   401	### 10.1 When to update this file
   402	
   403	- After architecture or boundary changes in any of:
   404	  - `src/services/veniceClient.ts`
   405	  - `server.ts`
   406	  - `electron/main.ts`
   407	  - `electron/ipc/*`
   408	  - release workflows
   409	  - shared validation/limits. `[VERIFIED]`
   410	- After changes to canonical scripts in `package.json`. `[VERIFIED]`
   411	- After new regression patterns appear (new `BUG-###` guards). `[VERIFIED]`
   412	
   413	### 10.2 How to update safely
   414	
   415	1. Run investigation pass first:
   416	   - `git log --oneline -50`
   417	   - `git log --since="6 months ago" --stat`
   418	   - `git log --pretty=format: --name-only | sort | uniq -c | sort -rn | head -20` `[VERIFIED]`
   419	2. Reconcile claims against source files and workflows.
   420	3. Tag claims:
   421	   - `[VERIFIED]` for directly observed facts.
   422	   - `[INFERRED]` for reasoned conclusions.
   423	4. If comparison to previous state is not proven in git history, state:
   424	   - `No structural change found in available history.` `[VERIFIED]`

     1	# Platform Support Matrix
     2	
     3	| OS | Architecture | Status | Packaging | Storage |
     4	|----|--------------|--------|-----------|---------|
     5	| Windows 10/11 | x64 | **Supported** | NSIS, Portable | DPAPI |
     6	| macOS 13+ | Apple Silicon (arm64) | **Supported** | DMG, ZIP | Keychain |
     7	| macOS 13+ | Intel (x64) | **Supported** | DMG, ZIP | Keychain |
     8	| Linux | x64 / arm64 | *Not officially packaged* | - | Plaintext Fallback (Dev Only) |

    11	### Known Limitations

    13	- Linux builds are intentionally excluded from `electron-builder` configs until an icon standard (`icon.png`) and smoke-testing workflow is implemented.

    53	- Associated `.sha256` checksums
    54	
    55	## Signing & Notarization
    56	
    57	### Windows
    58	Signing is optional for local development. Configure electron-builder-compatible signing with `CSC_LINK`/`CSC_KEY_PASSWORD` or `WIN_CSC_LINK`/`WIN_CSC_KEY_PASSWORD` for distribution. Unsigned builds may trigger SmartScreen.
    59	
    60	### macOS
    61	Local builds are ad-hoc signed. To distribute, you must configure macOS code signing (using `CSC_LINK` and `CSC_KEY_PASSWORD` containing a Developer ID Application certificate) and submit the build to Apple's notary service using notarization parameters. Unsigned/ad-hoc signed builds will trigger Gatekeeper warnings unless stripped of their quarantine flags via `xattr -dr com.apple.quarantine`.
    62	
    63	## GitHub Actions
    64	
    65	Use `.github/workflows/windows-release.yml` and `.github/workflows/macos-release.yml` for Windows and macOS builds.
    66	
    67	Triggers:
    68	- Manual `workflow_dispatch`
    69	- Version tags matching `v*`
    70	
    71	The workflows run `npm ci`, typecheck, tests, build, packaging commands (`dist:win` or `dist:mac`), checksum generation, and verification scripts (`verify:dist`), then upload the signed/unsigned bundles as release assets.
    72	
    73	## Smoke Test
    74	
    75	- [ ] Fresh launch routes to API key setup when no key exists.
    76	- [ ] Save, test, and delete API key.
    77	- [ ] Invalid key returns a clean `401`/`403` style message.
    78	- [ ] Model refresh succeeds after a valid key is saved.
    79	- [ ] Chat and image generation work.
    80	- [ ] Batch run completes successfully.
    81	- [ ] Research (web search, scrape, text-parser) returns results.
    82	- [ ] Export data creates versioned JSON without secrets.
    83	- [ ] Import validates and merges data without clearing existing records; pre-import backup saved to disk.
    84	- [ ] Copy diagnostics redacts secrets.
    85	- [ ] Open logs folder works.
    86	- [ ] Setup installer installs and uninstalls without deleting user data.
    87	- [ ] Portable exe launches without installation.
    88	- [ ] `verify:dist:portable` passes (`Venice-Forge-<version>-x64-Portable.exe` + `.sha256`).
    89	- [ ] SHA-256 checksum files match the final uploaded `.exe` files.
    90	- [ ] Release notes state whether artifacts are signed or unsigned.
    91	- [ ] Legal/TOS notes in [LEGAL.md](LEGAL.md) still link to current Venice pages.
    92	
    93	## Publish
    94	
    95	1. Create a tag: `git tag v<version> && git push origin v<version>`.

<!-- call_id: tool_w5lFlnyoSwBStQ7m12Esduf9 -->
```json
{
  "path": "docs/THEME_SYSTEM.md",
  "content": "# Venice Forge Theme System\n\n> Scope: Complete token-based theming architecture, live theme editor, FOUC prevention, and WCAG AA contrast compliance.\n> Implemented: 2026-05-28\n> Commit: `715fa1d`\n\n---\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n1. [Overview](#overview)\n2. [Architecture](#architecture)\n3. [Token Reference](#token-reference)\n4. [Built-in Themes](#built-in-themes)\n5. [ThemeMaker UI](#thememaker-ui)\n6. [Persistence & Lifecycle](#persistence--lifecycle)\n7. [Accessibility](#accessibility)\n8. [Adding a New Theme](#adding-a-new-theme)\n9. [File Inventory](#file-inventory)\n10. [Migration Notes](#migration-notes)\n\n---\n\n## Overview\n\nVenice Forge uses a **semantic token-based theme system** built on Tailwind CSS v4 CSS variables. Every color, border, shadow, and focus ring in the UI derives from a centralized set of 17 semantic tokens mapped to CSS custom properties. This enables:\n\n- **Built-in themes:** Forge Graphite (dark), Forge Daylight (light), Forge Copper (dark).\n- **Custom themes:** Users can define every token via the in-app ThemeMaker.\n- **Live preview:** Changes apply immediately without reload.\n- **Persistent storage:** Canonical settings live in encrypted IndexedDB; a lightweight `localStorage` bootstrap cache prevents FOUC on startup.\n- **WCAG AA compliance:** Contrast ratios are verified programmatically for all built-in themes and warned for custom themes.\n\n---\n\n## Architecture\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  Theme State (React reducer)                                │\n│  ├─ selectedThemeId: string                                 │\n│  ├─ appearanceMode: \"dark\" | \"light\"                        │\n│  └─ customTheme: Theme | null                               │\n│                          │                                  │\n│                          ▼                                  │\n│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────┐          │\n│  │  resolveInitialTheme(bootstrapCache?)         │          │\n│  │  → picks builtin / custom / prefers-color     │          │\n│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────┘          │\n│                          │                                  │\n│                          ▼                                  │\n│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────┐          │\n│  │  applyTheme(theme)                            │          │\n│  │  → writes CSS variables to :root              │          │\n│  │  → sets data-theme-mode on <html>             │          │\n│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────┘          │\n│                          │                                  │\n│                          ▼                                  │\n│  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────┐          │\n│  │  Tailwind v4 @theme                          │          │\n│  │  → maps CSS vars to utility classes          │          │\n│  │    (bg-bg, text-text-primary, border-border) │          │\n│  └──────────────────────────────────────────────┘          │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n### Two-Layer Persistence\n\n| Layer | Storage | Content | Purpose |\n|-------|---------|---------|---------|\n| **Canonical** | IndexedDB (`StorageService.saveItem(\"settings\", …)`) | Full `AppSettings` including `selectedThemeId`, `appearanceMode`, `customTheme` | Source of truth; encrypted at rest for `\"settings\"` store |\n| **Bootstrap** | `localStorage['vf.theme.bootstrap']` | Color tokens + metadata only (no secrets) | FOUC prevention; read by inline `<script>` in `index.html` before React mounts |\n\nAfter IndexedDB hydrates, `App.tsx` reconciles the canonical settings against the bootstrap cache. If they differ, the canonical theme is re-applied and the cache is refreshed.\n\n---\n\n## Token Reference\n\nThere are **17 semantic tokens**. Each maps to a CSS custom property (`--*`) and a Tailwind v4 utility class.\n\n| Token | CSS Variable | Tailwind Class | Role |\n|-------|-------------|----------------|------|\n| `background` | `--bg` | `bg-bg` | App/workspace background |\n| `surface` | `--surface` | `bg-surface` | Card/panel backgrounds |\n| `surfaceElevated` | `--surface-elevated` | `bg-surface-elevated` | Elevated cards, inputs, modal backdrops |\n| `border` | `--border` | `border-border` | Dividers, input borders |\n| `textPrimary` | `--text-primary` | `text-text-primary` | Headings, primary body text |\n| `textSecondary` | `--text-secondary` | `text-text-secondary` | Labels, secondary text |\n| `textMuted` | `--text-muted` | `text-text-muted` | Placeholders, hints, disabled text |\n| `accent` | `--accent` | `bg-accent`, `text-accent`, `border-accent` | Primary action color |\n| `accentHover` | `--accent-hover` | `hover:bg-accent-hover` | Accent hover state |\n| `accentForeground` | `--accent-fg` | `text-accent-fg` | Text on accent backgrounds (buttons, badges) |\n| `success` | `--success` | `text-success`, `border-success` | Positive status, success toasts |\n| `warning` | `--warning` | `text-warning`, `border-warning` | Cautions, warnings |\n| `danger` | `--danger` | `text-danger`, `border-danger` | Errors, destructive actions |\n| `info` | `--info` | `text-info` | Informational hints |\n| `focusRing` | `--focus-ring` | `focus-visible:ring-focus-ring` | Keyboard focus outline |\n| `overlay` | `--overlay` | `bg-overlay` | Modal/drawer backdrop scrim |\n| `glow` | `--glow` | `shadow-glow` | Accent glow on active elements |\n\n### Raw Hex Rule\n\nRaw hex values are intentionally **scoped** to:\n- `src/theme/themes.ts` — built-in palette definitions\n- `src/index.css` — brand palette, button gradients, scrollbar rgba\n- `src/components/ThemeMaker.tsx` — input fallback `#000000`\n- Test fixtures\n\nAll component and module bodies consume **CSS variables / Tailwind semantic tokens** only.\n\n---\n\n## Built-in Themes\n\n### Forge Graphite (dark) — `builtin-dark`\nThe default dark theme. Graphite base with Venice blue accent.\n\n### Forge Daylight (light) — `builtin-light`\nLight counterpart with a blue accent.\n\n### Forge Copper (dark) — `builtin-copper`\nDark graphite base with a copper accent for warm contrast.\n\n### Contrast Verification\n\n| Pair | Graphite | Daylight | Copper |\n|------|----------|----------|--------|\n| textPrimary / background | **16.02:1** | **14.84:1** | — |\n| textSecondary / surface | **7.08:1** | **6.39:1** | — |\n| accentForeground / accent | **4.90:1** | **5.19:1** | **5.03:1** |\n\nAll ratios exceed WCAG AA thresholds (4.5:1 for normal text, 3:1 for large text).\n\n---\n\n## ThemeMaker UI\n\nLocated in **Settings → Appearance → Theme Maker** (`src/components/ThemeMaker.tsx`).\n\n### Features\n- **Theme selector:** Switch between Forge Graphite, Forge Daylight, Forge Copper, or Custom.\n- **Token editor:** Each token has a synced native color picker and hex text input.\n- **Hex validation:** Regex `/^#([0-9a-f]{3}|[0-9a-f]{6})$/i`; invalid input falls back to `#000000`.\n- **Live preview:** `applyTheme(draftTheme)` updates the entire app in real time as you edit.\n- **Contrast warnings:** Checks `textPrimary/bg`, `textSecondary/surface`, and `accentForeground/accent` against WCAG AA. Warnings render in an `aria-live=\"polite\"` region.\n- **Preview card:** A mini app mock-up (`ThemePreview.tsx`) showing background, sidebar, active tab, button, input, and alert tokens.\n\n### Controls\n- **Save custom theme:** Persists to canonical IndexedDB settings + refreshes bootstrap cache.\n- **Reset custom theme:** Reverts editor to last saved custom theme.\n- **Restore defaults:** Switches to Forge Graphite and clears the custom theme.\n\n---\n\n## Persistence & Lifecycle\n\n### Startup (FOUC Prevention)\n\n1. Browser parses `index.html`.\n2. Inline `<script>` runs before paint:\n   - Reads `localStorage.getItem('vf.theme.bootstrap')`.\n   - If valid, applies CSS variables directly to `:root`.\n   - If missing/invalid, falls back to Forge Graphite (dark) or Forge Daylight (light) based on `prefers-color-scheme`.\n3. React mounts; `App.tsx` bootstraps.\n\n### Hydration\n\n1. `App.tsx` opens IndexedDB via `StorageService.openDB()`.\n2. Fetches settings with `getItemsWithMeta(\"settings\")`.\n3. Finds record `id === \"app-settings\"`.\n4. Dispatches `SET_SETTINGS` with stored settings (including theme fields).\n5. Post-dispatch `useEffect` reads `state.settings.selectedThemeId`, `appearanceMode`, `customTheme` → calls `applyTheme()`.\n\n### Reconciliation\n\nA separate `useEffect` in `App.tsx` compares canonical settings to the bootstrap cache. If drifted:\n- Re-applies the canonical theme.\n- Re-writes `localStorage['vf.theme.bootstrap']` with a colors-only snapshot.\n\n### Save\n\nA debounced (500 ms) `useEffect` on `state.settings` changes calls:\n```ts\nStorageService.saveItem(\"settings\", {\n  id: \"app-settings\",\n  value: state.settings,\n  timestamp: Date.now(),\n});\n```\n\n---\n\n## Accessibility\n\n- **Keyboard focus:** All interactives use `focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-focus-ring` with `--focus-ring` token.\n- **Reduced motion:** `src/index.css` includes `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)` rules.\n- **Aria-live:** Existing `aria-live=\"polite\"` regions (offline banner, status block, toast host, chat module, batch module, image generation form) were preserved. ThemeMaker adds an additional `aria-live=\"polite\"` region for contrast warnings.\n- **Color independence:** UI does not rely on color alone; status chips combine color tokens with border and background patterns.\n\n---\n\n## Adding a New Theme\n\n### Option A: Built-in Theme\n\n1. Open `src/theme/themes.ts`.\n2. Add a new `Theme` object:\n   ```ts\n   export const BUILTIN_OCEAN: Theme = {\n     id: \"builtin-ocean\",\n     name: \"Forge Ocean\",\n     mode: \"dark\",\n     tokens: { /* 17 tokens */ },\n   };\n   ```\n3. Export it from `src/theme/index.ts`.\n4. Add it to the theme list in `ThemeMaker.tsx`.\n5. Update the fallback map in `index.html` bootstrap script.\n6. Run contrast verification: `npx tsx -e \"import {contrastRatio} from './src/theme/contrast'; console.log(contrastRatio('#fff', '#0a0a0a'));\"`.\n7. Update this document.\n\n### Option B: Custom Theme at Runtime\n\nUsers create custom themes via the ThemeMaker UI. No code changes required.\n\n---\n\n## File Inventory\n\n### New Files\n\n| File | Purpose |\n|------|---------|\n| `src/theme/themeTypes.ts` | Type contracts (`ThemeMode`, `ThemeTokens`, `Theme`, `ThemeState`) |\n| `src/theme/themes.ts` | Built-in palette definitions |\n| `src/theme/applyTheme.ts` | Maps tokens to CSS variables + resolves initial theme |\n| `src/theme/contrast.ts` | WCAG luminance and contrast ratio utilities |\n| `src/theme/fallbacks.ts` | Shared fallback constant (`#000000`) for validation |\n| `src/theme/index.ts` | Barrel export |\n| `src/components/ThemeMaker.tsx` | Theme editor UI |\n| `src/components/ThemePreview.tsx` | Mini preview card |\n\n### Modified Files (Theming Impact)\n\n| File | Change |\n|------|--------|\n| `src/types/app.ts` | Extended `AppSettings` with theme fields |\n| `src/state/appReducer.ts` | Added theme fields to `initialState.settings` and `SET_SETTINGS` whitelist |\n| `src/index.css` | Expanded `:root` vars, `@theme` semantic colors, `.btn` system, `prefers-reduced-motion` |\n| `index.html` | Inline FOUC-prevention bootstrap script |\n| `src/App.tsx` | Theme hydration/reconciliation effects; reskinned shell |\n| `src/components/TabButton.tsx` | Token-based active/inactive states |\n| `src/components/Chip.tsx` | Token-based status chips |\n| `src/components/ToastHost.tsx` | Token-based toast variants |\n| `src/components/StatusBlock.tsx` | Token-based status indicators |\n| `src/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx` | Token-based error UI |\n| `src/components/ConfirmModal.tsx` | Token-based modal |\n| `src/components/Field.tsx` | Token-based form field |\n| `src/components/CollapsibleSection.tsx` | Token-based collapsible |\n| `src/components/ModelSelect.tsx` | Token-based dropdown |\n| `src/components/DiagnosticsPreview.tsx` | Token-based preview |\n| `src/components/ImageGenerationForm.tsx` | Token-based form |\n| `src/components/ImageGenerationPreview.tsx` | Token-based preview |\n| `src/components/ImageActionModal.tsx` | Token-based modal |\n| `src/modules/SettingsModule.tsx` | Integrated ThemeMaker; reskinned settings UI |\n| `src/modules/ChatModule.tsx` | Reskinned chat UI |\n| `src/modules/BatchModule.tsx` | Reskinned batch UI |\n| `src/modules/SearchScrapeModule.tsx` | Reskinned research UI |\n| `src/modules/GalleryModule.tsx` | Reskinned gallery UI |\n| `src/modules/ImageModule.tsx` | Reskinned image UI |\n| `src/modules/ModelsModule.tsx` | Reskinned models UI |\n| `src/modules/DiagnosticsModule.tsx` | Reskinned diagnostics UI |\n\n---\n\n## Migration Notes\n\n### For Contributors\n\n- **No `tailwind.config`:** Tailwind v4 is CSS-first. Add new semantic colors to the `@theme` block in `src/index.css`, not a JS config.\n- **No raw hex in components:** If you need a new color, add it as a token. If it is one-off, justify it in the PR. The existing exceptions are intentional and scoped.\n- **Test contrast:** If you change a built-in palette, run the contrast checks. The minimum acceptable ratio is 4.5:1 for text-on-background pairs.\n\n### For Users Upgrading from Pre-Theme Versions\n\n- On first launch after upgrade, the app detects no theme settings and defaults to **Forge Graphite (dark)**.\n- Existing settings (API key, model defaults, etc.) are preserved.\n- The old `theme` string field (if present) is migrated gracefully; the new fields `selectedThemeId`, `appearanceMode`, and `customTheme` take precedence.\n\n---\n\n## Further Reading\n\n- [`docs/ABOUT.md`](ABOUT.md) — Architecture and goals\n- [`docs/FAQ.md`](FAQ.md) — Frequently asked questions (includes theme Q&A)\n- [`CHANGELOG.md`](../CHANGELOG.md) — Version history\n- [`src/theme/`](../src/theme/) — Source code\n"
}
```

Introduce narrow `VeniceModel` interface, replace `any[]` initializers with `[]`, and break the circular dependency by extracting `AppState` shape into a standalone interface.\n  - **Effort:** Medium (2–4 hours, touches `appReducer.ts`, `types/app.ts`, `types/venice.ts`, and all module casts)\n\n### Suspected / Needs Verification\n\n- [ ] **[BUG-042 follow-up]** Symlink traversal in `isAllowedAppNavigation`\n  - **Status:** `fs.realpathSync` added with try/catch, but no automated test verifies symlink escape is blocked.\n  - **Fix:** Add unit test creating a symlink in `dist/` pointing outside the repo and asserting navigation is rejected.\n  - **Effort:** Low (30 min)\n\n- [ ] **[BUG-043 follow-up]** macOS ZIP artifact naming\n  - **Status:** `zip.artifactName` added to config to align with verify script, but a full `npm run dist:mac` has not been executed to confirm actual filenames.\n  - **Fix:** Run a local macOS build and inspect `release/*.zip` names, or rely on CI to validate.\n  - **Effort:** Low (requires macOS environment)\n\n### Theme System — Known Limitations & Enhancements\n\n- [ ] **[THEME-R001]** Bootstrap script duplication\n  - **What:** The inline `<script>` in `index.html` duplicates a subset of token fallback logic from `src/theme/applyTheme.ts`.\n  - **Risk:** If built-in palette colors change, the fallback map in `index.html` may drift.\n  - **Fix:** Generate the fallback map at build time from `src/theme/themes.ts` via a Vite plugin, or import a JSON manifest.\n  - **Effort:** Medium\n\n- [ ] **[THEME-R002]** Light mode edge-case audit\n  - **What:** Some legacy elements may still assume dark backgrounds (e.g. colored badges on colored backgrounds, hardcoded `shadow-black` equivalents).\n  - **Fix:** Systematic visual audit of all modules in Forge Daylight mode; replace any remaining dark assumptions.\n  - **Effort:** Low–Medium (1–2 hours)\n\n- [ ] **[THEME-R003]** Additional built-in themes\n  - **What:** Only three themes exist. Users may want more variety (e.g. high-contrast, solarized, nord, dracula).\n  - **Fix:** Add community-friendly palettes; ensure all pass WCAG AA.\n  - **Effort:** Low per theme\n\n- [ ] **[THEME-R004]** Theme export/import\n  - **What:** Custom themes are persisted in IndexedDB as part of settings, but the Export/Import flow does not explicitly surface or validate theme objects.\n  - **Fix:** Verify that `customTheme` round-trips correctly through export/import; add schema validation for `Theme` shape in `exportImport.ts` if missing.\n  - **Effort:** Low (30 min)\n\n- [ ] **[THEME-R005]** Per-mode custom themes\n  - **What:** Currently one `customTheme` object. Users may want separate custom dark and custom light themes.\n  - **Fix:** Extend `ThemeState` to `customThemeDark`/`customThemeLight` or add a `mode` field to custom themes.\n  - **Effort:** Medium (touches reducer, ThemeMaker UI, settings shape)\n\n- [ ] **[THEME-R006]** `prefers-contrast` support\n  - **What:** No high-contrast or reduced-transparency variants.\n  - **Fix:** Add `prefers-contrast: more` and `prefers-contrast: less` media query overrides in `src/index.css`.\n  - **Effort:** Low\n\n### Performance & Runtime\n\n- [ ] **[PERF-001]** `ThemeMaker` re-renders the entire app on every token change\n  - **What:** `applyTheme(draftTheme)` mutates `:root` CSS variables directly, which is fast, but React still re-renders the ThemeMaker component on every keystroke.\n  - **Fix:** Debounce hex input changes (e.g. 50 ms) or use `useDeferredValue` for the preview.\n  - **Effort:** Low\n\n- [ ] **[PERF-002]** `localStorage` bootstrap write on every settings change\n  - **What:** `App.tsx` writes `vf.theme.bootstrap` whenever `state.settings` changes, even for non-theme fields.\n  - **Fix:** Only write when theme-relevant fields change.\n  - **Effort:** Low (1-line `useEffect` dependency tweak)\n\n### Testing Gaps\n\n- [ ] **[TEST-001]** No unit tests for `applyTheme` or `resolveInitialTheme`\n  - **Fix:** Add `src/theme/contrast.test.ts` with known-good WCAG pairs (black/white, blue/white) and edge cases.\n  - **Effort:** Low (15 min)\n\n- [ ] **[TEST-003]** No unit tests for `ThemeMaker` or `ThemePreview`\n  - **Fix:** Add React Testing Library tests for theme selection, hex validation, and contrast warning display.\n  - **Effort:** Medium (1–2 hours)\n\n- [ ] **[TEST-004]** Electron smoke test is still minimal\n  - **Status:** Enhanced in BUG-038, but still does not verify window creation, preload injection, or IPC reachability.\n  - **Fix:** Add Playwright or Spectron-based smoke tests, or at least verify `window.veniceForge` is injected.\n  - **Effort:** High (requires new dependency or native module)\n\n### Documentation Gaps\n\n- [ ] **[DOC-R001]** `docs/THEME_SYSTEM.md` needs continuous updates\n  - **Action:** Whenever a new built-in theme is added or token set changes, update this file.\n  - **Owner:** Future contributors\n\n- [ ] **[DOC-R002]** `docs/REPOSITORY_TREE.md` may drift\n  - **Action:** Re-run `tree` or manual audit before each release to ensure file listings match reality.\n  - **Effort:** Low (automate with `tree -I 'node_modules|dist|dist-electron|release|.git'`)\n\n- [ ] **[DOC-R003]** `AGENT_REINITIALIZATION.md` pinned versions may stale\n  - **Action:** After any dependency update, refresh the lockfile-grounded version table in section 6.1.\n  - **Effort:** Low\n\n### Security & Hardening\n\n- [ ] **[SEC-R001]** Content Security Policy (CSP) does not mention `unsafe-inline` for the bootstrap script\n  - **What:** The inline script in `index.html` may violate a strict CSP if one is enforced.\n  - **Fix:** Either move the bootstrap to an external `.js` file, or ensure the CSP hash/nonce covers it. Verify in `electron/main.ts` CSP string.\n  - **Effort:** Low\n\n- [ ] **[SEC-R002]** `VENICE_FORGE_DEBUG_DEVTOOLS` bypass is not logged\n  - **What:** Enabling devtools in production is a security-relevant event but produces no audit log.\n  - **Fix:** Log a warning to the main-process logger when `VENICE_FORGE_DEBUG_DEVTOOLS=true` is detected.\n  - **Effort:** Low\n\n### Refactoring Debt\n\n- [ ] **[REFACTOR-001]** `App.tsx` is 348 lines and handles too many concerns\n  - **What:** Hydration, theme lifecycle, network status, bridge init, routing, and settings save all live in one file.\n  - **Fix:** Extract hooks: `useThemeLifecycle`, `useNetworkStatus`, `useSettingsPersistence`.\n  - **Effort:** Medium (2–3 hours)\n\n- [ ] **[REFACTOR-002]** Module props pattern is inconsistent\n  - **What:** Some modules take `{ state, dispatch }`; others may take additional props. No enforced contract.\n  - **Fix:** Introduce a `ModuleProps` type alias in `src/types/app.ts` and apply it uniformly.\n  - **Effort:** Low–Medium (1 hour)\n\n- [ ] **[REFACTOR-003]** `src/index.css` is large and mixes concerns\n  - **What:** Tailwind `@theme`, global styles, button system, scrollbar theming, reduced-motion, and FOUC prevention all in one file.\n  - **Fix:** Split into `src/styles/theme.css`, `src/styles/components.css`, `src/styles/global.css` and import them from `index.css`.\n  - **Effort:** Low (1 hour, mostly file moves)\n\n---\n\n## Quick Wins (effort <30 min • impact: Medium+)\n\n| ID | Task | File(s) |\n|----|------|---------|\n| QW-01 | Add `applyTheme.test.ts` | `src/theme/applyTheme.test.ts` |\n| QW-02 | Add `contrast.test.ts` | `src/theme/contrast.test.ts` |\n| QW-03 | Restrict bootstrap cache writes to theme-field changes only | `src/App.tsx` |\n| QW-04 | Add `prefers-contrast: more` media query overrides | `src/index.css` |\n| QW-05 | Log devtools bypass event | `electron/main.ts` |\n| QW-06 | Automate repo tree generation in release checklist | `docs/RELEASE/release.md` |\n| QW-07 | Add symlink escape unit test | `electron/main.ts` or new test file |\n\n---\n\n## Notes\n\n- `npm audit` returned 0 known dependency vulnerabilities at last scan.\n- The `dangerouslySetInnerHTML` in `src/utils/markdown.tsx` is **not** an XSS vulnerability because `escapeHtml` runs before all regex replacements.\n- All `aria-live` regions from before the theme work were preserved; no regressions in screen-reader behavior.\n- One unrelated pre-existing diff exists in `src/modules/ChatModule.test.tsx` (BUG-051 regression guard) — outside theme scope and should be committed separately.\n"

     1	/** @fileoverview Global application reducer and state helpers for Venice Forge. */
     2	
     3	import { FALLBACK_MODELS, DEFAULT_SYSTEM_PROMPT } from "../constants/venice";

     8	/**
     9	 * Determines the model category from its metadata.
    10	 *
    11	 * @param model Raw model object from the API.
    12	 * @returns The inferred category, e.g. "text", "image", or "unknown".
    13	 */
    14	function classifyModel(model: any) {
    15	  const id = String(model.id || model.model || "").toLowerCase();
    16	  const type = String(
    17	    model.type || model.model_type || model.modelType || ""
    18	  ).toLowerCase();
    19	  const traits = JSON.stringify(
    20	    model.traits || model.capabilities || model.features || {}
    21	  ).toLowerCase();
    22	
    23	  if (["text", "llm", "chat", "code"].includes(type)) return "text";
    24	  if (["image", "inpaint", "upscale"].includes(type)) return "image";
    25	  if (["tts", "asr", "audio", "music"].includes(type)) return "audio";
    26	  if (type === "video") return "video";
    27	  if (["embedding", "embeddings"].includes(type)) return "embeddings";
    28	
    29	  if (/embed/.test(id + traits)) return "embeddings";
    30	  if (/image|sdxl|flux|fluently|lustify|pony|stable|diffusion|inpaint|upscale|banana/.test(id + traits))
    31	    return "image";
    32	  if (/audio|voice|speech|tts|asr|transcri|music/.test(id + traits)) return "audio";
    33	  if (/video|wan|motion|animate/.test(id + traits)) return "video";
    34	  if (/llama|qwen|deepseek|mistral|grok|dolphin|venice|chat|text|coder|reason|zai|glm|kimi|gemma|gemini|hermes|openai/.test(id + traits))
    35	    return "text";
    36	  return "unknown";
    37	}
    38	
    39	/**
    40	 * Normalizes a raw model list into grouped categories.
    41	 *
    42	 * @param payload Raw API response or array of models.
    43	 * @returns Record mapping categories to arrays of normalized models.
    44	 */
    45	export function flattenModels(payload: any) {
    46	  const list = Array.isArray(payload?.data)
    47	    ? payload.data
    48	    : Array.isArray(payload)
    49	    ? payload
    50	    : [];
    51	  const groups: Record<string, any[]> = {
    52	    text: [],
    53	    image: [],
    54	    audio: [],
    55	    video: [],
    56	    embeddings: [],
    57	    unknown: [],
    58	  };
    59	  list.forEach((m: any) => {
    60	    const normalized = {
    61	      ...m,
    62	      id: m.id || m.model || m.name || "unknown-model",
    63	      name: m.name || m.display_name || m.id || m.model || "unknown model",
    64	      type: m.type || m.model_type || m.modelType || classifyModel(m),
    65	      isFallback: false,
    66	      source: "live" as const,
    67	    };
    68	    groups[classifyModel(normalized)].push(normalized);
    69	  });
    70	  return groups;
    71	}
    72	
    73	/**
    74	 * Injects fallback models into empty category groups.
    75	 *
    76	 * @param groups Model groups from flattenModels.
    77	 * @returns A new groups object with fallback models where needed.
    78	 */
    79	export function withFallbackModels(groups: Record<string, any[]>) {
    80	  const next: Record<string, any[]> = {
    81	    text: [],
    82	    image: [],
    83	    audio: [],
    84	    video: [],
    85	    embeddings: [],
    86	    unknown: [],
    87	    ...groups,
    88	  };
    89	  if (!next.text.length) next.text = FALLBACK_MODELS.text;
    90	  if (!next.image.length) next.image = FALLBACK_MODELS.image;
    91	  return next;
    92	}

    94	/**
    95	 * Coerces a web search setting to a canonical value.
    96	 *
    97	 * @param value Raw setting value, which may be a boolean or string.
    98	 * @returns The normalized setting: "off", "on", or "auto".
    99	 */
   100	function normalizeWebSearchSetting(value: unknown): "off" | "on" | "auto" {
   101	  if (value === true) return "on";
   102	  if (value === false) return "off";
   103	  if (value === "off" || value === "on" || value === "auto") return value;
   104	  warn("normalizeWebSearchSetting: invalid value, defaulting to off", value);
   105	  return "off";
   106	}

   165	/**
   166	 * Applies an action to the application state.
   167	 *
   168	 * @param state The current immutable state.
   169	 * @param action The dispatched action.
   170	 * @returns The next immutable state.
   171	 */
   172	export const appReducer = produce((draft: typeof initialState, action: AppAction) => {
   173	  switch (action.type) {
   174	    case "SET_TAB":
   175	      draft.activeTab = action.tab;
   176	      break;
   177	    case "SET_MODELS": {
   178	      const models = withFallbackModels(action.models || {});
   179	      draft.models = models;
   180	      draft.usingFallbackModels = !!action.fallback;
   181	
   182	      const chatModelExists = models.text.some((m: any) => m.id === draft.selectedChatModel);
   183	      const imageModelExists = models.image.some((m: any) => m.id === draft.selectedImageModel);
   184	
   185	      if (!chatModelExists) {
   186	        const firstLive = models.text.find((m: any) => m.source === "live");
   187	        const fallback = models.text[0];
   188	        draft.selectedChatModel = firstLive?.id || fallback?.id || "venice-uncensored";
   189	        if (draft.selectedChatModel) {
   190	          draft.toasts.push({
   191	            id: crypto.randomUUID(),
   192	            message: `Previous chat model was unavailable. Switched to ${draft.selectedChatModel}.`,
   193	            type: "warn",
   194	            duration: 6000,
   195	          });
   196	        }
   197	      }
   198	
   199	      if (!imageModelExists) {
   200	        const firstLive = models.image.find((m: any) => m.source === "live");
   201	        const fallback = models.image[0];
   202	        draft.selectedImageModel = firstLive?.id || fallback?.id || "flux-dev";
   203	        if (draft.selectedImageModel) {
   204	          draft.toasts.push({
   205	            id: crypto.randomUUID(),
   206	            message: `Previous image model was unavailable. Switched to ${draft.selectedImageModel}.`,
   207	            type: "warn",
   208	            duration: 6000,
   209	          });
   210	        }
   211	      }
   212	
   213	      draft.modelLoadError = action.error || "";
   214	      break;
   215	    }
   216	    case "SET_SELECTED_CHAT_MODEL":
   217	      draft.selectedChatModel = action.model;
   218	      break;
   219	    case "SET_SELECTED_IMAGE_MODEL":
   220	      draft.selectedImageModel = action.model;
   221	      break;
   222	    case "SET_SETTINGS": {
   223	      // Defensive: ignore non-object payloads that could crash the `in` operator.
   224	      if (!action.settings || typeof action.settings !== "object" || Array.isArray(action.settings)) break;
   225	      // Explicit property whitelist to prevent prototype pollution.
   226	      const allowedKeys: (keyof typeof draft.settings)[] = [
   227	        "defaultSystemPrompt", "includeVeniceSystemPrompt", "webSearch", "webScraping", "webCitations", "theme", "customModels",
   228	        "selectedThemeId", "appearanceMode", "customTheme",
   229	      ];
   230	      for (const key of allowedKeys) {
   231	        if (key in action.settings) {
   232	          const nextValue = (action.settings as Record<string, unknown>)[key];
   233	          if (key === "defaultSystemPrompt") {
   234	            if (typeof nextValue === "string") draft.settings.defaultSystemPrompt = nextValue;
   235	            continue;
   236	          }
   237	          if (key === "includeVeniceSystemPrompt") {
   238	            if (typeof nextValue === "boolean") draft.settings.includeVeniceSystemPrompt = nextValue;
   239	            continue;
   240	          }
   241	          if (key === "webSearch") {
   242	            draft.settings.webSearch = normalizeWebSearchSetting(nextValue);
   243	            continue;
   244	          }
   245	          if (key === "webScraping") {
   246	            if (typeof nextValue === "boolean") draft.settings.webScraping = nextValue;
   247	            continue;
   248	          }
   249	          if (key === "webCitations") {
   250	            if (typeof nextValue === "boolean") draft.settings.webCitations = nextValue;
   251	            continue;
   252	          }
   253	          if (key === "theme") {
   254	            if (nextValue === "dark" || nextValue === "light" || nextValue === "system") {
   255	              draft.settings.theme = nextValue;
   256	            }
   257	            continue;
   258	          }
   259	          if (key === "customModels") {
   260	            if (Array.isArray(nextValue)) {
   261	              draft.settings.customModels = nextValue.filter((m: unknown): m is string => typeof m === "string");
   262	            }
   263	            continue;
   264	          }
   265	          if (key === "selectedThemeId") {
   266	            if (typeof nextValue === "string") draft.settings.selectedThemeId = nextValue;
   267	            continue;
   268	          }
   269	          if (key === "appearanceMode") {
   270	            if (nextValue === "dark" || nextValue === "light") draft.settings.appearanceMode = nextValue;
   271	            continue;
   272	          }
   273	          if (key === "customTheme") {
   274	            if (nextValue === null || (typeof nextValue === "object" && "id" in (nextValue as object) && "tokens" in (nextValue as object))) {
   275	              draft.settings.customTheme = nextValue as import("../theme/themeTypes").Theme | null;
   276	            }
   277	            continue;
   278	          }
   279	        }
   280	      }
   281	      break;
   282	    }
   283	    case "SET_DIAGNOSTICS": {
   284	      const entry = {
   285	        ...action.diagnostics,
   286	        id: crypto.randomUUID(),
   287	        timestamp: Date.now(),
   288	      };
   289	      draft.diagnostics = entry;
   290	      draft.diagnosticsLog.unshift(entry);
   291	      if (draft.diagnosticsLog.length > 50) {
   292	        draft.diagnosticsLog.pop();
   293	      }
   294	      break;
   295	    }
   296	    case "SET_GALLERY":
   297	      draft.gallery = action.items || [];
   298	      break;
   299	    case "SET_CHATS":
   300	      draft.chats = action.items || [];
   301	      break;
   302	    case "TOGGLE_SOURCE_PANEL":
   303	      draft.sourcePanelOpen = !draft.sourcePanelOpen;
   304	      break;
   305	    case "SET_CHAT_DRAFT":
   306	      if (action.patch && typeof action.patch === "object") {
   307	        Object.assign(draft.chatDraft, action.patch);
   308	      }
   309	      break;
   310	    case "SET_IMAGE_DRAFT":
   311	      if (action.patch && typeof action.patch === "object") {
   312	        Object.assign(draft.imageDraft, action.patch);
   313	      }
   314	      break;
   315	    case "SET_BATCH_DRAFT":
   316	      if (action.patch && typeof action.patch === "object") {
   317	        Object.assign(draft.batchDraft, action.patch);
   318	      }
   319	      break;
   320	    case "SET_ONLINE":
   321	      draft.isOnline = action.online;
   322	      break;
   323	    case "ADD_TOAST":
   324	      draft.toasts.push(action.toast);
   325	      break;
   326	    case "REMOVE_TOAST":
   327	      draft.toasts = draft.toasts.filter((t) => t.id !== action.id);
   328	      break;
   329	  }
   330	});

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

Let me analyze the BUG-020 issue:

1. `classifyModel(model: any)` - takes `any`, but we can define a `RawVeniceModel` interface
2. `flattenModels(payload: any)` - takes `any`, returns `Record<string, any[]>`
3. `withFallbackModels(groups: Record<string, any[]>)` - takes/returns `any[]`
4. State initializers use `any`:
   - `diagnostics: null as any`
   - `diagnosticsLog: [] as any[]`
   - `gallery: [] as any[]`
   - `chats: [] as any[]`
   - `imageDraft.currentImages: [] as any[]`

The `AppState = typeof initialState` circular dependency means `AppState` depends on `initialState`, and `initialState` uses type imports from `app.ts` (which imports `AppState`). This is actually not a circular dependency in the module graph since TypeScript type imports are erased, but it creates a circular *type* dependency.

The fix strategy:
1. Define `RawVeniceModel` in `src/types/venice.ts` - a loose interface for API model objects
2. Define `ModelGroups` properly in `src/types/venice.ts` 
3. Replace `any` in `appReducer.ts` state initializers with proper types
4. Fix the circular type dependency by either:
   - Moving `AppState` and `AppAction` to a separate types file that doesn't import `initialState`
   - Or defining `AppState` as an explicit interface instead of `typeof initialState`

Actually, looking at `src/types/app.ts`:
```ts
import { initialState } from "../state/appReducer";
export type AppState = typeof initialState;
```

And `src/state/appReducer.ts` imports from `src/types/app.ts`:
```ts
import type { AppAction } from "../types/app";
```

This IS a circular module dependency. In TypeScript, `import type` is erased at runtime, but it can still cause issues with the compiler. Let me check if this actually causes problems.

The current state works because:
- `appReducer.ts` does `import type { AppAction } from "../types/app"` (type-only)
- `app.ts` does `import { initialState } from "../state/appReducer"` (value import)

This creates a circular dependency graph. At runtime it works because `import type` is erased. But for type-checking, TypeScript resolves it.

The real fix for BUG-020 is:
1. Define `RawVeniceModel` and update `ModelInfo` or create a separate type
2. Replace all `any[]` in state with proper types
3. Break the circular dependency by defining `AppState` as an explicit interface

For the explicit interface approach, I would define `AppState` directly in `src/types/app.ts` without importing `initialState`. But then I need to keep them in sync.

Alternatively, I can define `AppState` in `appReducer.ts` and export it from there, then `app.ts` imports it. But then `appReducer.ts` still needs `AppAction` from `app.ts`.

Actually, the cleanest approach is:
1. Keep `AppAction` in `app.ts`
2. Define `AppState` as an explicit interface in `app.ts` (not `typeof initialState`)
3. Make `initialState` in `appReducer.ts` satisfy `AppState` by adding a type annotation
4. This breaks the circular dependency

But this is a big change. Let me look at what the todo says:
"requires coordinated model-type refactor. Introduce narrow VeniceModel interface, replace any[] initializers with [], and break the circular dependency by extracting AppState shape into a standalone interface."

Actually, `ModelInfo` already exists in `src/types/venice.ts` but it's very minimal. The API returns more fields than that. Let me create a `RawVeniceModel` type that's more flexible.

For the state initializers:
- `diagnostics: null as any` → should be `DiagnosticsEntry | null`
- `diagnosticsLog: [] as any[]` → should be `DiagnosticsEntry[]`
- `gallery: [] as any[]` → should be `GalleryImage[]`

```ts
/** Metadata for a single model returned by the Venice API. */
export interface ModelInfo {
  id: string;
  created?: number;
  object?: string;
  owned_by?: string;
  name?: string;
```

Wait, I shouldn't make `ModelInfo` too loose because it loses type safety. Let me instead create a new type hierarchy:

```ts
/** Raw model object as returned by the Venice API (before normalization). */
export interface RawVeniceModel {
  id?: string;
  model?: string;
  name?: string;
  display_name?: string;
  type?: string;
  model_type?: string;
  modelType?: string;
  traits?: unknown;
  capabilities?: unknown;
  features?: unknown;
  [key: string]: unknown;
}

/** Normalized model used throughout the application. */
export interface NormalizedModel {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: string;
  isFallback: boolean;
  source: "live" | "fallback";
  traits?: unknown;
}
```

And keep `ModelInfo` as-is for backward compatibility, but update `ModelGroups` to use `NormalizedModel` and update `ModelSelect` to accept `NormalizedModel[]`.

```ts
models: ModelInfo[];
```
And it only accesses `m.id`. So either `ModelInfo` or `NormalizedModel` works.

Actually, the simplest approach: just update `ModelInfo` to include the fields the app needs, since the current `ModelInfo` is clearly incomplete (only 4 fields). The Venice API returns much more than that.

Let me check what the actual Venice API returns for models...

Actually, I don't need to be perfectly accurate to the API. I just need types that match what the app code expects. Let me define a practical `ModelInfo`:

```ts
export interface ModelInfo {
  id: string;
  name?: string;
  type?: string;
  traits?: unknown;
  isFallback?: boolean;
  source?: "live" | "fallback" | string;
  // Raw API fields
  created?: number;
  object?: string;
  owned_by?: string;
  model?: string;
  display_name?: string;
  model_type?: string;
  modelType?: string;
  capabilities?: unknown;
  features?: unknown;
}
```

This is loose but practical. It allows the app to use the fields it needs while accepting the raw API response.

Actually, for better type safety, let me separate concerns:
- `ModelInfo` stays as the OpenAI-style interface (minimal, for API compatibility)
- `NormalizedModel` is what the app creates after `flattenModels`

Then `ModelSelect` can accept `(ModelInfo | NormalizedModel)[]` or just `Array<{ id: string }>`. But that's overkill.

Let me just keep it simple: update `ModelInfo` to be practical. The app doesn't need strict OpenAI compatibility since it's a Venice-specific client.

For the state initializers, I need:
- `diagnostics: null as any` → `null as DiagnosticsEntry | null`
- `diagnosticsLog: [] as any[]` → `[] as DiagnosticsEntry[]`
- `gallery: [] as any[]` → `[] as GalleryImage[]`
- `chats: [] as any[]` → `[] as ChatRecord[]`
- `imageDraft.currentImages: [] as any[]` → `[] as GalleryImage[]`

For the reducer:
- `draft: typeof initialState` → `draft: AppState`
- `const chatModelExists = models.text.some((m: any) => m.id === draft.selectedChatModel);` → remove `: any`
- Same for other `: any` annotations in the reducer

For `flattenModels`:
```ts
export function flattenModels(payload: unknown): Record<string, NormalizedModel[]> {
```

And `withFallbackModels`:
```ts
export function withFallbackModels(groups: Record<string, NormalizedModel[]>): Record<string, NormalizedModel[]> {
```

Wait, but `FALLBACK_MODELS` in `venice.ts` returns objects with `isFallback: true, source: "fallback"` but not all the `NormalizedModel` fields. Specifically, `NormalizedModel` would require `name: string` and `type: string`, but the fallback objects have those. Good.

Let me also check what `withFallbackModels` returns. It does:
```ts
next.text = FALLBACK_MODELS.text;
```

So `FALLBACK_MODELS.text` objects need to satisfy `NormalizedModel`. They have `id`, `type`, `name`, `isFallback`, `source`. Good.

OK, let me now implement all the changes. I'll do them in parallel where possible.

This should become:

<details><summary>Thinking</summary>

Now let me fix the `flattenModels` function in `appReducer.ts`. The issue is that `list.forEach((m) => { ... })` has `m` as `unknown` because `list` is `unknown[]`. I need to type `m` as `ModelInfo` or use a type assertion.

Also, the payload handling:
```ts
const raw = payload as Record<string, unknown> | unknown[] | undefined;
const list = Array.isArray(raw?.data)
  ? (raw.data as unknown[])
  : Array.isArray(raw)
  ? raw
  : [];
```

The problem is `raw?.data` - when `raw` is `unknown[]`, `raw.data` doesn't exist. But `Array.isArray(raw?.data)` would be false for arrays, so it would fall through to `Array.isArray(raw)`. But TypeScript doesn't narrow properly here because `raw?.data` is evaluated on a union type.

Let me rewrite this more cleanly:
```ts
export function flattenModels(payload: unknown): Record<string, ModelInfo[]> {
  let list: unknown[] = [];
  if (payload && typeof payload === "object") {
    if (Array.isArray(payload)) {
      list = payload;
    } else if ("data" in payload && Array.isArray((payload as Record<string, unknown>).data)) {
      list = (payload as Record<string, unknown>).data as unknown[];
    }
  }
  const groups: Record<string, ModelInfo[]> = { ... };
  list.forEach((m) => {
    const item = m as ModelInfo;
    const normalized = { ...item, ... };
    ...
  });
  return groups;
}
```

Actually, let me think about this more carefully. The issue with `raw?.data` on a union is that TypeScript sees `raw` as `Record<string, unknown> | unknown[] | undefined`. When we do `raw?.data`, for the `unknown[]` branch, `.data` doesn't exist. But the optional chaining makes it `undefined`, and `Array.isArray(undefined)` is false, so it falls through. TypeScript should be able to narrow this, but apparently it can't because of the union.

Let me restructure:
```ts
export function flattenModels(payload: unknown): Record<string, ModelInfo[]> {
  let list: unknown[] = [];
  if (Array.isArray(payload)) {
    list = payload;
  } else if (payload && typeof payload === "object" && "data" in payload && Array.isArray((payload as Record<string, unknown>).data)) {
    list = (payload as Record<string, unknown>).data as unknown[];
  }
  ...
}
```

For the `forEach`:
```ts
  list.forEach((m) => {
    const item = m as Record<string, unknown>;
    const normalized: ModelInfo = {
      ...item,
      id: String(item.id || item.model || "unknown-model"),
      name: String(item.name || item.display_name || item.id || item.model || "unknown model"),
      type: String(item.type || item.model_type || item.modelType || classifyModel(item as ModelInfo)),
      isFallback: false,
      source: "live",
    };
    groups[classifyModel(normalized)].push(normalized);
  });
```

Wait, `classifyModel` takes `ModelInfo`, but `item` is `Record<string, unknown>`. I can cast `item as ModelInfo` for `classifyModel`. But `classifyModel` accesses fields like `model.id`, `model.model`, `model.type` etc. which may be undefined. Since `ModelInfo` has them all as optional, that's fine.

Actually, looking at the current code:
```ts
list.forEach((m: any) => {
  const normalized = {
    ...m,
    id: m.id || m.model || m.name || "unknown-model",
    name: m.name || m.display_name || m.id || m.model || "unknown model",
    type: m.type || m.model_type || m.modelType || classifyModel(m),
    isFallback: false,
    source: "live" as const,
  };
  groups[classifyModel(normalized)].push(normalized);
});
```

The issue is that `m` is now `unknown`. I need to cast it. Let me use `Record<string, unknown>` as an intermediate:

```ts
list.forEach((raw) => {
  const m = raw as Record<string, unknown>;
  const normalized: ModelInfo = {
    ...(m as Record<string, unknown>),
    id: String(m.id || m.model || m.name || "unknown-model"),
    name: String(m.name || m.display_name || m.id || m.model || "unknown model"),
    type: String(m.type || m.model_type || m.modelType || classifyModel(m as ModelInfo)),
    isFallback: false,
    source: "live",
  };
  groups[classifyModel(normalized)].push(normalized);
});
```

Actually, spreading `m` when it's `Record<string, unknown>` should work since `ModelInfo` extends that.

Now for the `action.models` type issue. In `AppAction`:
```ts
| { type: "SET_MODELS"; models: Record<string, unknown[]> | undefined; fallback?: boolean; error?: string }
```

This should be:
```ts
| { type: "SET_MODELS"; models: Record<string, ModelInfo[]> | undefined; fallback?: boolean; error?: string }
```

But `AppAction` is in `src/types/app.ts` which doesn't import `ModelInfo`... Actually it uses `import("./venice").ModelInfo` in `AppState`, so I can do the same in `AppAction`.

Now for the `DiagnosticsEntry` issue:
```ts
case "SET_DIAGNOSTICS": {
  const entry = {
    ...action.diagnostics,
    id: crypto.randomUUID(),
    timestamp: Date.now(),
  };
  draft.diagnostics = entry;
```

`action.diagnostics` is `Partial<DiagnosticsEntry>`, so spreading it creates an object that might not have `type`. But `DiagnosticsEntry` requires `type`. I need to add a default or make the spread produce a full `DiagnosticsEntry`.

```ts
const entry: DiagnosticsEntry = {
  type: "info",
  endpoint: "",
  status: null,
  latencyMs: null,
  ...action.diagnostics,
  id: crypto.randomUUID(),
  timestamp: Date.now(),
};
```

This ensures all required fields are present, with overrides from `action.diagnostics`.

For `SET_CHATS`:
```ts
| { type: "SET_CHATS"; items: Array<Record<string, unknown>> }
```

<system>104 lines read from file starting from line 1. Total lines in file: 104. End of file reached.</system>
     1	/** @fileoverview Fetches and caches the Venice model catalog with stale-while-revalidate behavior. */
     2	
     3	import { veniceFetch } from "./veniceClient";
     4	import { flattenModels } from "../state/appReducer";
     5	import { isValidModelListResponse } from "../utils/veniceValidation";
     6	import { warn } from "../shared/logger";
     7	import type { AppDispatch } from "../types/app";
     8	
     9	/** localStorage key for the model cache. */
    10	const CACHE_KEY = "venice-forge-models-cache";
    11	
    12	/** Cache time-to-live in milliseconds (5 minutes). */
    13	const CACHE_TTL_MS = 5 * 60 * 1000;
    14	
    15	/** Shape of the persisted model cache entry. */
    16	interface ModelsCache {
    17	  grouped: Record<string, unknown[]>;
    18	  fetchedAt: number;
    19	  isStale?: boolean;
    20	}
    21	
    22	function isValidGroupedModels(value: unknown): boolean {
    23	  if (!value || typeof value !== "object" || Array.isArray(value)) return false;
    24	  const grouped = value as Record<string, unknown>;
    25	  const requiredKeys = ["text", "image", "audio", "video", "embeddings", "unknown"];
    26	  return requiredKeys.every((key) => Array.isArray(grouped[key]));
    27	}
    28	
    29	/**
    30	 * Reads the model cache from localStorage, marking it stale if expired.
    31	 * @returns The cached data, or null if missing or unreadable.
    32	 */
    33	function readCache(): ModelsCache | null {
    34	  try {
    35	    const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(CACHE_KEY);
    36	    if (!raw) return null;
    37	    const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
    38	    if (!parsed || typeof parsed !== "object") return null;
    39	    if (!isValidGroupedModels(parsed.grouped)) return null;
    40	    if (typeof parsed.fetchedAt !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(parsed.fetchedAt)) return null;
    41	    const isStale = Date.now() - parsed.fetchedAt > CACHE_TTL_MS;
    42	    return { ...parsed, isStale };
    43	  } catch {
    44	    return null;
    45	  }
    46	}
    47	
    48	/**
    49	 * Writes grouped model data to localStorage.
    50	 * @param grouped The model groups to cache.
    51	 */
    52	function writeCache(grouped: Record<string, unknown[]>): void {
    53	  try {
    54	    window.localStorage.setItem(CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify({ grouped, fetchedAt: Date.now() }));
    55	  } catch (err) {
    56	    warn("[modelService] Failed to cache models in localStorage:", err);
    57	  }
    58	}
    59	
    60	/**
    61	 * Refreshes the model catalog, serving cached data immediately when available.
    62	 * @param dispatch The app dispatch function for state updates.
    63	 * @param force If true, bypasses the freshness check and always refreshes.
    64	 * @returns A promise that resolves once the refresh attempt completes.
    65	 */
    66	export async function refreshModels(dispatch: AppDispatch, force = false): Promise<void> {
    67	  const cached = readCache();
    68	
    69	  // Serve cached data immediately (even if stale) to reduce perceived latency.
    70	  if (cached) {
    71	    dispatch({ type: "SET_MODELS", models: cached.grouped, fallback: false });
    72	    const isStale = !!cached.isStale;
    73	    if (!force && !isStale) {
    74	      return; // Fresh — no background refresh needed.
    75	    }
    76	    // Stale or forced: fall through to background refresh while cached UI is already shown.
    77	  }
    78	
    79	  try {
    80	    const { data } = await veniceFetch("/models?type=all", {
    81	      method: "GET",
    82	      dispatch,
    83	      retry: true,
    84	      dedupe: true,
    85	    });
    86	    if (!isValidModelListResponse(data)) {
    87	      throw new Error("Unexpected /models response shape.");
    88	    }
    89	    const grouped = flattenModels(data);
    90	    writeCache(grouped);
    91	    dispatch({ type: "SET_MODELS", models: grouped, fallback: false });
    92	  } catch (err: unknown) {
    93	    // If we already served cached data, swallow the error silently.
    94	    if (!cached) {
    95	      const message = (err as { message?: string })?.message;
    96	      dispatch({
    97	        type: "SET_MODELS",
    98	        models: undefined,
    99	        fallback: true,
   100	        error: message || "Model discovery failed; using non-exhaustive static fallbacks.",
   101	      });
   102	    }
   103	  }
   104	}

The `modelService.ts` has `ModelsCache` with `grouped: Record<string, unknown[]>`. When it dispatches `SET_MODELS` with `cached.grouped`, the type is `Record<string, unknown[]>`, but `AppAction` now expects `Record<string, ModelInfo[]>`. 

I need to update `ModelsCache` to use `Record<string, ModelInfo[]>`. But since `readCache()` parses JSON and doesn't validate item types deeply, I should cast the parsed grouped data.

Actually, the simplest fix: update `ModelsCache` and `writeCache` to use `Record<string, ModelInfo[]>`, and cast in `readCache` when returning.

```ts
interface ModelsCache {
  grouped: Record<string, ModelInfo[]>;
  fetchedAt: number;
  isStale?: boolean;
}

function writeCache(grouped: Record<string, ModelInfo[]>): void {
```

```ts
return { ...parsed, grouped: parsed.grouped as Record<string, ModelInfo[]>, isStale };
```
